životopis</span></button></div></div></div></div><div class="_7a133"><p></p><h2>Full stack web developer in Zeni team s.r.o. - remote work</h2><p></p><p>Do you want to be a part of a dynamic international team in a growing company? Do you like to organize your own time and learn new things? Are you ready to roll up your sleeves when needed? Are front and back-end programming something you excel at and enjoy working on? Then we have good news for you: In Zeni team, we are looking for a colleague who would like to join us!</p><p></p><p><b>Job description, responsibilities and duties</b></p><p></p><p>In cooperation with our team you will work on the development of themes and plugins in WordPress. </p><p></p><p>We are open, so you can come up with your creativity and ideas, that you can devop. </p><p></p><p>We expect independence at your work but of course we help each other. </p><p></p><p><b>Whats benefits to be a part of the Zeni team?</b></p><p></p><p>Enjoy open hands for your work</p><p></p><p>Full home office, remote work</p><p></p><p>Flexible working hours</p><p></p><p>Gross salary 1500+/month according to your experience for position</p><p></p><p>Career growth opportunity</p><p></p><p>Make coffee in quite office near the airport in Brno</p><p></p><p>Work in an international team with a fast-paced company culture based on respect</p><p></p><p>Continuous professional learning and growing in languages and technical skills</p><p></p><p><b>Employee requirements</b></p><p></p><p>General knowledge of technologies</p><p></p><p>2+ years of full-stack web programming experience</p><p></p><p>Advanced experience in PHP 7.x, HTML5, (S)CSS, JavaScript</p><p></p><p>Knowledge of WordPress programming both themes and plugins</p><p></p><p>Experience with React, Node.js</p><p></p><p><b>Language skills</b></p><p></p><p>English - B2 </p><p></p><p><b>Other knowledge</b></p><p></p><p>Analytical thinking </p><p></p><p>Ability to solve tasks independently</p><p></p><p>Interested in learning new technologies </p><p></p><p>Proactive approach in solving tasks</p><p></p><p>Practical knowledge of GIT, MVC</p><p></p><p><b>Personality requirements and skills</b></p><p></p><p>Independence at work</p><p></p><p>Interested in learning new things</p><p></p><p>Flexibility</p><p></p><p>Communication skills for team work</p><p></p><p>Being a team player when it comes to help your colleagues and brainstorming for new developments</p><p></p><p><b>Information about the selection process</b></p><p></p><p>Thank you for your interest! The selection process will be in two rounds. First, please send us your current CV and you can also send us an interesting project that you have worked on or participated in. After reviewing your CV, we will contact you. We will schedule an online interview with candidates whose qualifications/experience matches our needs to find out more information. </p><p></p><p><b>Brief characteristics of the company</b></p><p></p><p>We are a company with 10 years of experience. Weve been building websites together since 2012. We create complete websites &amp; eCommerce solutions and we develop WordPress plugins &amp; themes. We have a relaxed culture reinforced by exceptional freelancers and other partners.</p><p></p><p>Our mission is to create websites that bring joy to both their owners and their users. We work at our own pace and style, allowing us to make our jobs purposeful and enjoyable. Thats how we stay at our best.
